\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Fill the whole Neo\+Pixel strip with 0 / black / off. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
void \mbox{\hyperlink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a74e917093c2eb16848c4a09427680f79}{update\+Length}} (uint16\+\_\+t n)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em 更改已声明的\+Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel灯带对象的长度。旧数据会被释放，新数据会被清空。 引脚号和像素格式不变。 \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
void \mbox{\hyperlink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a07b6949674125159484e9e02ef025f7d}{update\+Type}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8h_ab88a50d51bb5488df4379ff49c81fd72}{neo\+Pixel\+Type}} t)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em 更改之前声明的像素格式 Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel灯带对象。如果格式从一个变为另一个 将\+RGB变体转换为\+RGBW变体（或将\+RGBW转换为\+RGB），旧的 数据将被释放，新数据将被清空。否则， 旧数据将保留在\+RAM中，并且不会重新排序到 由于是新格式，建议随后执行 \doxylink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_ae259682b202be0acd258d6879f4c7121}{clear()} 操作。 \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
bool \mbox{\hyperlink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a9e900a60b0ac2b43b99309bb118b929e}{can\+Show}} (void)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Check whether a call to \doxylink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a4bcda7a15591065570d3598cbf970be7}{show()} will start sending data immediately or will \textquotesingle{}block\textquotesingle{} for a required interval. Neo\+Pixels require a short quiet time (about 300 microseconds) after the last bit is received before the data \textquotesingle{}latches\textquotesingle{} and new data can start being received. Usually one\textquotesingle{}s sketch is implicitly using this time to generate a new frame of animation...but if it finishes very quickly, this function could be used to see if there\textquotesingle{}s some idle time available for some low-\/priority concurrent task. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_ab484e9a9da6f1089091c2cda1a0841a7}{get\+Pixels}} (void) const
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Get a pointer directly to the Neo\+Pixel data buffer in RAM. Pixel data is stored in a device-\/native format (a la the NEO\+\_\+\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} constants) and is not translated here. Applications that access this buffer will need to be aware of the specific data format and handle colors appropriately. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
uint8\+\_\+t \mbox{\hyperlink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_ab1b7af02712d6a1e228783a89ec12832}{get\+Brightness}} (void) const

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Class that stores state and functions for interacting with Adafruit Neo\+Pixels and compatible devices.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Adafruit\_NeoPixel()}{Adafruit\_NeoPixel()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a2a7ab8a0cedee029cd5330b638146ccc} 
Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel\+::\+Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



“空”\+Neo\+Pixel构造函数，当长度、引脚和/或像素类型在编译时未知， 需后续用update\+Type()、update\+Length()和set\+Pin()初始化。 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel对象。使用前需调用begin()函数。 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
此函数已弃用，仅为兼容旧项目。新项目应使用第一个构造函数语法（长度、引脚、类型）。 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a9e900a60b0ac2b43b99309bb118b929e}\index{Adafruit\_NeoPixel@{Adafruit\_NeoPixel}!canShow@{canShow}}
\index{canShow@{canShow}!Adafruit\_NeoPixel@{Adafruit\_NeoPixel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{canShow()}{canShow()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a9e900a60b0ac2b43b99309bb118b929e} 
bool Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel\+::can\+Show (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Check whether a call to \doxylink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a4bcda7a15591065570d3598cbf970be7}{show()} will start sending data immediately or will \textquotesingle{}block\textquotesingle{} for a required interval. Neo\+Pixels require a short quiet time (about 300 microseconds) after the last bit is received before the data \textquotesingle{}latches\textquotesingle{} and new data can start being received. Usually one\textquotesingle{}s sketch is implicitly using this time to generate a new frame of animation...but if it finishes very quickly, this function could be used to see if there\textquotesingle{}s some idle time available for some low-\/priority concurrent task. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 or true if \doxylink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a4bcda7a15591065570d3598cbf970be7}{show()} will start sending immediately, 0 or false if \doxylink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a4bcda7a15591065570d3598cbf970be7}{show()} would block (meaning some idle time is available). 
\end{DoxyReturn}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8h_source_l00257}{257}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8h_source}{Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel.\+h}}.

uint32\+\_\+t Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel\+::\+Color (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{r}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{g}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{b}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}

\end{DoxyReturn}

uint32\+\_\+t Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel\+::\+Color (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{r}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{g}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{b}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{w}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a1f16aee5b96e16e62598f826e292b23b}\index{Adafruit\_NeoPixel@{Adafruit\_NeoPixel}!ColorHSV@{ColorHSV}}
\index{ColorHSV@{ColorHSV}!Adafruit\_NeoPixel@{Adafruit\_NeoPixel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ColorHSV()}{ColorHSV()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a1f16aee5b96e16e62598f826e292b23b} 
uint32\+\_\+t Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel\+::\+Color\+HSV (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{hue}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{sat}{ = {\ttfamily 255}, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{val}{ = {\ttfamily 255}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Convert hue, saturation and value into a packed 32-\/bit RGB color that can be passed to \doxylink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_ab8763ccc6f9a090df1f753905fd5561e}{set\+Pixel\+Color()} or other RGB-\/compatible functions. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em hue} & An unsigned 16-\/bit value, 0 to 65535, representing one full loop of the color wheel, which allows 16-\/bit hues to "{}roll               over"{} while still doing the expected thing (and allowing more precision than the wheel() function that was common to prior Neo\+Pixel examples). \\
\hline
{\em sat} & Saturation, 8-\/bit value, 0 (min or pure grayscale) to 255 (max or pure hue). Default of 255 if unspecified. \\
\hline
{\em val} & Value (brightness), 8-\/bit value, 0 (min / black / off) to 255 (max or full brightness). Default of 255 if unspecified. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Packed 32-\/bit RGB with the most significant byte set to 0 -- the white element of WRGB pixels is NOT utilized. Result is linearly but not perceptually correct, so you may want to pass the result through the \doxylink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a0151163f5aeaa42676bc31a978d6d666}{gamma32()} function (or your own gamma-\/correction operation) else colors may appear washed out. This is not done automatically by this function because coders may desire a more refined gamma-\/correction function than the simplified one-\/size-\/fits-\/all operation of \doxylink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a0151163f5aeaa42676bc31a978d6d666}{gamma32()}. Diffusing the LEDs also really seems to help when using low-\/saturation colors. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{fill()}{fill()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a310844b3e5580056edf52ce3268d8084} 
void Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel\+::fill (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{c}{ = {\ttfamily 0}, }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{first}{ = {\ttfamily 0}, }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{count}{ = {\ttfamily 0}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Fill all or part of the Neo\+Pixel strip with a color. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c} & 32-\/bit color value. Most significant byte is white (for RGBW pixels) or ignored (for RGB pixels), next is red, then green, and least significant byte is blue. If all arguments are unspecified, this will be 0 (off). \\
\hline
{\em first} & Index of first pixel to fill, starting from 0. Must be in-\/bounds, no clipping is performed. 0 if unspecified. \\
\hline
{\em count} & Number of pixels to fill, as a positive value. Passing 0 or leaving unspecified will fill to end of strip. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{gamma32()}{gamma32()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a0151163f5aeaa42676bc31a978d6d666} 
uint32\+\_\+t Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel\+::gamma32 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



A gamma-\/correction function for 32-\/bit packed RGB or WRGB colors. Makes color transitions appear more perceptially correct. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em x} & 32-\/bit packed RGB or WRGB color. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Gamma-\/adjusted packed color, can then be passed in one of the \doxylink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_ab8763ccc6f9a090df1f753905fd5561e}{set\+Pixel\+Color()} functions. Like \doxylink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_ab932cb619cd3420f9e3f269b7401710e}{gamma8()}, this uses a fixed gamma correction exponent of 2.\+6, which seems reasonably okay for average Neo\+Pixels in average tasks. If you need finer control you\textquotesingle{}ll need to provide your own gamma-\/correction function instead. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

An 8-\/bit gamma-\/correction function for basic pixel brightness adjustment. Makes color transitions appear more perceptially correct. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em x} & Input brightness, 0 (minimum or off/black) to 255 (maximum). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

If you need finer control you\textquotesingle{}ll need to provide your own gamma-\/correction function instead.

uint32\+\_\+t Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel\+::get\+Pixel\+Color (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{n}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}



Query the color of a previously-\/set pixel. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em n} & Index of pixel to read (0 = first). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\textquotesingle{}Packed\textquotesingle{} 32-\/bit RGB or WRGB value. Most significant byte is white (for RGBW pixels) or 0 (for RGB pixels), next is red, then green, and least significant byte is blue. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If the strip brightness has been changed from the default value of 255, the color read from a pixel may not exactly match what was previously written with one of the \doxylink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_ab8763ccc6f9a090df1f753905fd5561e}{set\+Pixel\+Color()} functions. This gets more pronounced at lower brightness levels. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_ab484e9a9da6f1089091c2cda1a0841a7}\index{Adafruit\_NeoPixel@{Adafruit\_NeoPixel}!getPixels@{getPixels}}
\index{getPixels@{getPixels}!Adafruit\_NeoPixel@{Adafruit\_NeoPixel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getPixels()}{getPixels()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_ab484e9a9da6f1089091c2cda1a0841a7} 
uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel\+::get\+Pixels (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Get a pointer directly to the Neo\+Pixel data buffer in RAM. Pixel data is stored in a device-\/native format (a la the NEO\+\_\+\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} constants) and is not translated here. Applications that access this buffer will need to be aware of the specific data format and handle colors appropriately. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Pointer to Neo\+Pixel buffer (uint8\+\_\+t\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} array). 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This is for high-\/performance applications where calling \doxylink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_ab8763ccc6f9a090df1f753905fd5561e}{set\+Pixel\+Color()} on every single pixel would be too slow (e.\+g. POV or light-\/painting projects). There is no bounds checking on the array, creating tremendous potential for mayhem if one writes past the ends of the buffer. Great power, great responsibility and all that. 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a914f61b78e4d36a03c91372ceded2d46} 
void Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel\+::rainbow (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{first\+\_\+hue}{ = {\ttfamily 0}, }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{reps}{ = {\ttfamily 1}, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{saturation}{ = {\ttfamily 255}, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{brightness}{ = {\ttfamily 255}, }\item[{bool}]{gammify}{ = {\ttfamily true}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



用一个或多个色调循环填充\+Neo\+Pixel灯带。 大家都非常喜欢彩虹漩涡，现在它可是经典了！ 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em first\+\_\+hue} & 第一个像素的色调，0-\/65535，表示一个完整的色调范围 色轮的循环。每个后续像素将 （能量/数据等）被抵消以完成一个或多个周期 条带的长度。 \\
\hline
{\em reps} & 在整个长度上色轮的循环次数 条带的宽度。默认值为1。负值可以 用于颠倒色调顺序。 \\
\hline
{\em saturation} & 饱和度（可选），0-\/255 表示从灰色到纯色调， 默认值 = 255。 \\
\hline
{\em brightness} & 亮度/值（可选），0-\/255 表示从关闭到最大亮度， 默认值 = 255。这是独特的，并且是结合使用的 具有任何配置的全局条带亮度。 \\
\hline
{\em gammify} & 如果为true（默认值），则对颜色应用伽马校正 为了提升外观。 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_aa05f7d37828c43fef00e6242dcf75959}\index{Adafruit\_NeoPixel@{Adafruit\_NeoPixel}!setBrightness@{setBrightness}}
\index{setBrightness@{setBrightness}!Adafruit\_NeoPixel@{Adafruit\_NeoPixel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBrightness()}{setBrightness()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_aa05f7d37828c43fef00e6242dcf75959} 
void Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel\+::set\+Brightness (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{b}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Adjust output brightness. Does not immediately affect what\textquotesingle{}s currently displayed on the LEDs. The next call to \doxylink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a4bcda7a15591065570d3598cbf970be7}{show()} will refresh the LEDs at this level. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em b} & Brightness setting, 0=minimum (off), 255=brightest. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This was intended for one-\/time use in one\textquotesingle{}s \doxylink{main_8cpp_a4fc01d736fe50cf5b977f755b675f11d}{setup()} function, not as an animation effect in itself. Because of the way this library "{}pre-\/multiplies"{} LED colors in RAM, changing the brightness is often a "{}lossy"{} operation -- what you write to pixels isn\textquotesingle{}t necessary the same as what you\textquotesingle{}ll read back. Repeated brightness changes using this function exacerbate the problem. Smart programs therefore treat the strip as a write-\/only resource, maintaining their own state to render each frame of an animation, not relying on read-\/modify-\/write. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a4bcda7a15591065570d3598cbf970be7}\index{Adafruit\_NeoPixel@{Adafruit\_NeoPixel}!show@{show}}
\index{show@{show}!Adafruit\_NeoPixel@{Adafruit\_NeoPixel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{show()}{show()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a4bcda7a15591065570d3598cbf970be7} 
void Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel\+::show (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



将\+RAM中的像素数据传输到\+Neo\+Pixels。 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
在大多数架构中，中断会被暂时禁用 为了实现正确的\+Neo\+Pixel信号时序。这意味着 Arduino的millis()和micros()函数，这两个函数需要 中断，每当发生这种情况时，都会损失一小段时间间隔 函数被调用（每个\+RGB像素大约30微秒，40个像素为 RGBW像素）。这个问题没有简单的解决办法，但有一些 存在使用...的专门替代库或配套库 需要使用非常针对特定设备的外设来解决这个问题。 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_afb00024000da81bcb6378c7052f77be3}\index{Adafruit\_NeoPixel@{Adafruit\_NeoPixel}!sine8@{sine8}}
\index{sine8@{sine8}!Adafruit\_NeoPixel@{Adafruit\_NeoPixel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sine8()}{sine8()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_afb00024000da81bcb6378c7052f77be3} 
uint8\+\_\+t Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel\+::sine8 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}



An 8-\/bit integer sine wave function, not directly compatible with standard trigonometric units like radians or degrees. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em x} & Input angle, 0-\/255; 256 would loop back to zero, completing the circle (equivalent to 360 degrees or 2 pi radians). One can therefore use an unsigned 8-\/bit variable and simply add or subtract, allowing it to overflow/underflow and it still does the expected contiguous thing. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Sine result, 0 to 255, or -\/128 to +127 if type-\/converted to a signed int8\+\_\+t, but you\textquotesingle{}ll most likely want unsigned as this output is often used for pixel brightness in animation effects. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a5cec6fe17e75f8d607df305e2fa9db5c}\index{Adafruit\_NeoPixel@{Adafruit\_NeoPixel}!str2order@{str2order}}
\index{str2order@{str2order}!Adafruit\_NeoPixel@{Adafruit\_NeoPixel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{str2order()}{str2order()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a5cec6fe17e75f8d607df305e2fa9db5c} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8h_ab88a50d51bb5488df4379ff49c81fd72}{neo\+Pixel\+Type}} Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel\+::str2order (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



将像素颜色顺序从字符串（例如“\+BGR”）转换为\+Neo\+Pixel格式 颜色顺序常量（例如 NEO\+\_\+\+BGR）。这可能对代码有所帮助 从文本配置进行初始化，而非编译时初始化 常数。 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em v} & 输入字符串。应进行合理净化（3位或4位） （以字符\+NUL结尾的字符串）或可能产生未定义行为 结果（输出仍然是一个有效的\+Neo\+Pixel指令常量，但 （结果）可能不会如预期呈现。输入垃圾，输出垃圾。 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
返回一个\+Neo\+Pixel颜色顺序常量（例如\+NEO\+\_\+\+BGR）。 NEO\+\_\+\+KHZ400或\+NEO\+\_\+\+KHZ800位既未包含在内，也不需要（全部 经发现，\+Neo\+Pixels实际上支持800 KHz，这就是 （若未设置\+KHZ位，则为默认状态）。 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
此函数在类中被声明为静态，因此可以调用它 没有\+Neo\+Pixel对象（因为它不太可能被声明） （尚未在代码中实现）。请使用\+Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel\+::str2order()函数。 
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{updateType()}{updateType()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a07b6949674125159484e9e02ef025f7d} 
void Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel\+::update\+Type (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8h_ab88a50d51bb5488df4379ff49c81fd72}{neo\+Pixel\+Type}}}]{t}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



更改之前声明的像素格式 Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel灯带对象。如果格式从一个变为另一个 将\+RGB变体转换为\+RGBW变体（或将\+RGBW转换为\+RGB），旧的 数据将被释放，新数据将被清空。否则， 旧数据将保留在\+RAM中，并且不会重新排序到 由于是新格式，建议随后执行 \doxylink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_ae259682b202be0acd258d6879f4c7121}{clear()} 操作。 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em t} & 像素类型 -- 将\+NEO\+\_\+\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}常量（在...中定义）相加 例如，在\+Adafruit\+\_\+\+Neo\+Pixel.\+h中，对于\+NEO\+\_\+\+GRB+NEO\+\_\+\+KHZ800 Neo\+Pixels期望接收800 KHz（而非400 KHz）的数据流 颜色字节以绿色、红色、蓝色的顺序表示像素。 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
此函数已弃用，此处仅用于旧项目 可能仍然在使用它。新项目应改用 “new”关键字与第一个构造函数的语法 （长度，引脚，类型）。 
\end{DoxyNote}
